## Analysis

The GT expression is:
$$0.2332 \cdot A^{1/3} - 0.3115 \cdot A^2 - 0.3115 \cdot A \cdot e^{-0.08476 \cdot t}$$

This has three terms: an $A^{1/3}$ term, an $A^2$ term, and an $A \cdot e^{ct}$ term (with no additive constant).

Let me check the candidates:

**Candidate 33**: $A^{1/3} c_0 + A^2 c_1 + A c_2 \exp(c_3 t)$

This has exactly three terms matching the GT structure:
- $c_0 = 0.2332$ for the $A^{1/3}$ term
- $c_1 = -0.3115$ for the $A^2$ term
- $c_2 = -0.3115$ for the $A \cdot \exp$ term
- $c_3 = -0.08476$ for the exponential decay rate

This is a perfect match with no extra constant term needed (and indeed the GT has no additive constant).

**Candidate 46**: $A^{1/3} c_0 + A^2 c_1 + A c_2 \exp(c_3 t) + c_4$

This also works by setting $c_4 = 0$.

**Candidate 48**: $A^{0.333333} c_0 + A^2 c_1 + A c_2 \exp(c_3 t) + c_4$

Same as 46 with explicit exponent, works with $c_4 = 0$.

**Candidate 47**: $A^{1/3} c_0 + A^2 c_1 + A^2 c_2 + A c_3 \exp(c_4 t) + c_5$

Works by combining $c_1 + c_2$ for the $A^2$ coefficient and setting $c_5 = 0$.

Many other candidates also work (e.g., candidates 5, 11, 4, 18, 19, 20, etc.) by setting extra parameters to 0 or combining terms appropriately.

The simplest and most direct match is **Candidate 33**: $A^{1/3} c_0 + A^2 c_1 + A c_2 \exp(c_3 t)$, which matches the GT exactly with:
- $c_0 = 0.2332$
- $c_1 = -0.3115$
